Remains to prove termination of a 42-rules system (42 strict rules).

Remains to prove termination of a 41-rules system (41 strict rules).
Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
Remains to prove termination of a 193-rules system (152 strict rules).
